## üîç Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### üéØ Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 9 page(s) - 9 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R4: Page has a descriptive title](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r4)
**Issue**: The `lang` attribute is either missing, empty, or only whitespace

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<html>...</html>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/html
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/html')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://www.comune.roma.it/
- https://minsk.gov.by/
- http://www.birmingham.gov.uk/
- http://www.tbilisi.gov.ge/
- https://omr.gov.ua/
- *...and 4 more page(s)*

#### Pattern 5: Affects 5 page(s) - 5 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [meta-refresh](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/meta-refresh?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical
**Issue**: Delayed refresh under 20 hours must not be used

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<meta http-equiv="refresh" content="360">
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
meta[http-equiv="refresh"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('meta[http-equiv="refresh"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://kyivcity.gov.ua/
- https://basra.gov.iq/
- http://dniprorada.gov.ua/
- https://frankfurt.de/
- https://www.bremen.de/

---

#### Pattern 9: Affects 3 page(s) - 3 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate
**Issue**: All page content should be contained by landmarks

**HTML Pattern**:
```html

```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):

#### Pattern 11: Affects 2 page(s) - 42 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R17: No description](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r17)
**Issue**: The element is either tabbable or has tabbable descendants

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<ul class="km1-main-nav__link-list km1-main-nav__link-list--level-2" data-js-main-nav-level="2" aria-hidden="true">...</ul>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/ul[@class="km1-main-nav__link-list km1-main-nav__link-list--level-2"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/ul[@class="km1-main-nav__link-list km1-main-nav__link-list--level-2"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://www.hamburg.de/
- https://www.hamburg.com/

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://www.london.gov.uk/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="ccc-notify-button ccc-link ccc-tabbable ccc-notify-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="u-u-group u-space-x-2" href="/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-u-group u-space-x-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="u-w-full btn btn--outline" href="/who-we-are">       View our who we are page   </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="u-w-full btn btn--outline"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/who-we-are/what-mayor-does">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/who-we-are/what-london-assembly-does">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

*... and 28 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R43](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r43)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg role="img" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The grouping element has an accessible name
- HTML: `<fieldset data-drupal-selector="edit-checkbox-mailchimp" id="edit-checkbox-mailchimp--wrapper" class="checkboxes--wrapper fieldgroup form-composite webform-composite-visible-title js-webform-type-checkboxes webform-type-checkboxes js-form-item form-item js-form-wrapper form-wrapper" aria-describedby="edit-checkbox-mailchimp--wrapper--description">...</fieldset>`

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

- HTML: `<p class="lead">...</p>`

- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<iframe title="reCAPTCHA" width="304" height="78" role="presentation" name="a-1on0owimi1j4" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" sandbox="allow-forms allow-popups allow-same-origin allow-scripts allow-top-navigation allow-modals allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox allow-storage-access-by-user-activation" src="https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api2/anchor?ar=1&k=6Ld5PzEUAAAAAG34guiPpNoqPmNKMdrvJaeJO5Zl&co=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubG9uZG9uLmdvdi51azo0NDM.&hl=en&type=image&v=vUgXt_KV952_-5BB2jjloYzl&theme=light&size=normal&anchor-ms=20000&execute-ms=30000&cb=yt5t47m9ytin" />`
- XPath: `/iframe`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://www.london.gov.uk/

#### Rule: [svg-img-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/svg-img-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: <svg> elements with an img role must have alternative text
- HTML: `<svg role="img" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="simple-icons-icon simple-icons-icon__linkedin" focusable="false">`
- XPath: `.simple-icons-icon__linkedin`

### https://www.berlin.de/

#### Rule: [color-contrast](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/color-contrast?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<p class="image__copyright">¬© contrastwerkstatt - stock.adobe.com</p>`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(1) > .tile[data-add-clickable-area="full"] > .image--darken.image > .image__overlay.align--bottom > .image__copyright`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<p class="image__copyright">¬© dpa</p>`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(2) > .tile[data-add-clickable-area="full"] > .image--darken.image > .image__overlay.align--bottom > .image__copyright`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<p class="image__copyright">¬© dpa</p>`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(3) > .tile[data-add-clickable-area="full"] > .image--darken.image > .image__overlay.align--bottom > .image__copyright`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<p class="image__copyright">¬© dpa</p>`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(4) > .tile[data-add-clickable-area="full"] > .image--darken.image > .image__overlay.align--bottom > .image__copyright`

#### Rule: [empty-heading](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/empty-heading?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Headings should not be empty
- HTML: `<h2 class="title heading-channel"></h2>`
- XPath: `#layout-grid__area--maincontent > .heading-channel`

#### Rule: [landmark-contentinfo-is-top-level](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-contentinfo-is-top-level?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Contentinfo landmark should not be contained in another landmark
- HTML: `<div id="content-footer" role="contentinfo">         <h2 class="aural">Weitere Informationen zu diesem Auftritt</h2>         <div class="content-footer__brand">         </div>         <a class="to-top" href="#top">Zum Seitenanfang</a>         <!-- content-footer__links empty -->       </div>`
- XPath: `#content-footer`

#### Rule: [landmark-no-duplicate-contentinfo](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-no-duplicate-contentinfo?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Document should not have more than one contentinfo landmark
- HTML: `<div id="content-footer" role="contentinfo">         <h2 class="aural">Weitere Informationen zu diesem Auftritt</h2>         <div class="content-footer__brand">         </div>         <a class="to-top" href="#top">Zum Seitenanfang</a>         <!-- content-footer__links empty -->       </div>`
- XPath: `#content-footer`

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<div id="content-footer" role="contentinfo">         <h2 class="aural">Weitere Informationen zu diesem Auftritt</h2>         <div class="content-footer__brand">         </div>         <a class="to-top" href="#top">Zum Seitenanfang</a>         <!-- content-footer__links empty -->       </div>`
- XPath: `#content-footer`

### https://www.madrid.es/

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<div class="navItem1" role="ElementosCarrousel0" tabindex="0" aria-label="Ver la primera diapo..." aria-controls="slide_1" aria-selected="true" onclick="paginacion1(this)" onkeyup="paginacion1Event(eve..." style="cursor: pointer; wid...">`
- XPath: `.navItem1`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<div class="navItem2" role="ElementosCarrousel1" tabindex="0" aria-label="Ver la segunda diapo..." aria-controls="slide_2" aria-selected="false" onclick="paginacion2(this)" onkeyup="paginacion2Event(eve..." style="cursor: pointer; wid...">`
- XPath: `.navItem2`

#### Rule: [aria-prohibited-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-prohibited-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use permitted ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<div class="navItem1" role="ElementosCarrousel0" tabindex="0" aria-label="Ver la primera diapo..." aria-controls="slide_1" aria-selected="true" onclick="paginacion1(this)" onkeyup="paginacion1Event(eve..." style="cursor: pointer; wid...">`
- XPath: `.navItem1`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements must only use permitted ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<div class="navItem2" role="ElementosCarrousel1" tabindex="0" aria-label="Ver la segunda diapo..." aria-controls="slide_2" aria-selected="false" onclick="paginacion2(this)" onkeyup="paginacion2Event(eve..." style="cursor: pointer; wid...">`
- XPath: `.navItem2`

#### Rule: [aria-required-children](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-required-children?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must contain particular children
- HTML: `<ul class="nav nav-tabs nav-tabs-type2" role="tablist">`
- XPath: `.nav-tabs-type2`

#### Rule: [aria-required-parent](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-required-parent?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must be contained by particular parents
- HTML: `<a href="#tab-para_ti" aria-controls="tab-para_ti" role="tab" data-toggle="tab">Para ti</a>`
- XPath: `a[href$="#tab-para_ti"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must be contained by particular parents
- HTML: `<a href="#tab-en_tu_distrito" aria-controls="tab-en_tu_distrito" role="tab" data-toggle="tab">En tu distrito</a>`
- XPath: `a[href$="#tab-en_tu_distrito"]`

#### Rule: [aria-roles](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-roles?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA roles used must conform to valid values
- HTML: `<div class="navItem1" role="ElementosCarrousel0" tabindex="0" aria-label="Ver la primera diapo..." aria-controls="slide_1" aria-selected="true" onclick="paginacion1(this)" onkeyup="paginacion1Event(eve..." style="cursor: pointer; wid...">`
- XPath: `.navItem1`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: ARIA roles used must conform to valid values
- HTML: `<div class="navItem2" role="ElementosCarrousel1" tabindex="0" aria-label="Ver la segunda diapo..." aria-controls="slide_2" aria-selected="false" onclick="paginacion2(this)" onkeyup="paginacion2Event(eve..." style="cursor: pointer; wid...">`
- XPath: `.navItem2`

#### Rule: [aria-valid-attr-value](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-valid-attr-value?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA attributes must conform to valid values
- HTML: `<div class="navItem1" role="ElementosCarrousel0" tabindex="0" aria-label="Ver la primera diapo..." aria-controls="slide_1" aria-selected="true" onclick="paginacion1(this)" onkeyup="paginacion1Event(eve..." style="cursor: pointer; wid...">`
- XPath: `.navItem1`

#### Rule: [image-redundant-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/image-redundant-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Alternative text of images should not be repeated as text
- HTML: `<img src="/UnidadesDescentralizadas/UDCMedios/noticias/2026/02Febrero/23Lunes/NotasdePrensa/AlmeidaSandboxMadrid/destacada2.jpeg" alt="Almeida asegura que ‚ÄúMadrid es el ecosistema adecuado para innovar, aprender y experimentar‚Äù durante la presentaci√≥n de Sandbox Madrid" class="info_relevant">`
- XPath: `.hightlight > .info_relevant_img > .info_relevant`

#### Rule: [listitem](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/listitem?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: <li> elements must be contained in a <ul> or <ol>
- HTML: `<li class="bg-tab_arrow first active col-md-3 col-sm-4 col-xs-6"><a href="#tab-para_ti" aria-controls="tab-para_ti" role="tab" data-toggle="tab">Para ti</a></li>`
- XPath: `.bg-tab_arrow`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: <li> elements must be contained in a <ul> or <ol>

- HTML: `<h5>–ü—Ä–æ –≤–Ω–µ—Å–µ–Ω–Ω—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω –¥–æ —Ä—ñ—à–µ–Ω–Ω—è –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω–∞–≤—á–æ–≥–æ –∫–æ–º—ñ—Ç–µ—Ç—É –ó–∞–ø–æ—Ä—ñ–∑—å–∫–æ—ó –º—ñ—Å—å–∫–æ—ó —Ä–∞–¥–∏ –≤—ñ–¥ 28.01.2016 ‚Ññ 9 ¬´–ü—Ä–æ —Å—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è –º—ñ—Å—Ü–µ–≤–æ—ó –∫–æ–º—ñ—Å—ñ—ó –∑ –ø–∏—Ç–∞–Ω—å —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–æ–≥–µ–Ω–Ω–æ-–µ–∫–æ–ª–æ–≥—ñ—á–Ω–æ—ó –±–µ–∑–ø–µ–∫–∏ —ñ –Ω–∞–¥–∑–≤–∏—á–∞–π–Ω–∏—Ö —Å–∏—Ç—É–∞—Ü—ñ–π –º. –ó–∞–ø–æ—Ä—ñ–∂–∂—è, –∑–∞—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–¥–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è —ó—ó —Å–∫–ª–∞–¥—É —Ç–∞ –ü–æ–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—è¬ª —É —Ä–µ–¥–∞–∫—Ü—ñ—ó –≤—ñ–¥ 18.07.2025</h5>`
- XPath: `.decisions-item:nth-child(2) > a > h5`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h4>                                 –•–∞—Ä—á–µ–Ω–∫–æ –†–µ–≥—ñ–Ω–∞ –í–ª–∞–¥–∏—Å–ª–∞–≤—ñ–≤–Ω–∞                             </h4>`
- XPath: `.council-item:nth-child(2) > h4`

#### Rule: [link-name](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/link-name?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Links must have discernible text
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.facebook.com/zaporizhzhiacitycouncil" target="_blank">`
- XPath: `.social-icons > a[target="_blank"]:nth-child(1)`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Links must have discernible text
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.instagram.com/zaporizhzhia_city_council/" target="_blank">`
- XPath: `a[target="_blank"]:nth-child(2)`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Links must have discernible text
- HTML: `<a href="https://t.me/zaporizhzhiacitycouncil" target="_blank">`
- XPath: `a[target="_blank"]:nth-child(3)`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Links must have discernible text
- HTML: `<a href="/rss.xml" target="_blank">`
- XPath: `a[href$="rss.xml"]`

### https://www.bremen.de/

#### Rule: [meta-refresh](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/meta-refresh?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Delayed refresh under 20 hours must not be used
- HTML: `<meta http-equiv="refresh" content="360">`
- XPath: `meta[http-equiv="refresh"]`
